 Azam Bhagat Singh is a name in the history of Indian freedom struggle without which the story of independence would have remained incomplete
 vah sirf yuvaaon hi nahin, balki bujurgon or bacchon ke bhi adarsh hai
 a 400-page diary written by him in Lahore Central Jail tells the story of his bird's personality
 vah lekhakon, rachanakaaron, itihaaskaaron or samajashastriyon sabake liye preranarot rahe hai
 Bhagat Singh is considered as Professor Chamanlal Krantiveer of Jawaharlal Nehru University and is also considered to be the leader of the ideological revolution
 unka kahana he ki maatr 23 saal kii umr main shahid ho jane vaale is yuva ke bina shaayad aazaadee kii kahani adhuri kehalaati
 Chamanlal in his book 'krantiveer Bhagat Singh: Abhyudaya and Bhavishya' has given a comprehensive description of the martyrdom, martyrdom and martyrdom of Shaheed A
 Azam
 unka kahana he ki yadi bhagat singh na hote to aaj desh ke liye shaayad koi aisa adarsh na hota jisane vaicharik kranti ke dam par aise shashan kii neenv hilaa di jiskaa samrajya duniyabar main failaa tha
 He told that after Bhagat Singh's hanging on March 23, 1931, India's journalism world was awash with news related to him
 shahid e ajam kii jeevani likhane ke liye jitendranath sanyaal ko gori hukumat ne do saal kaid kii sajaa sunai thi
